Task instruction sent to agent 
# Bug Investigation: Dark Mode Text Threshold Setting Has No Effect on Qt 6.4

**Repository:** qutebrowser/qutebrowser
**Task Type:** Find and Prove (write a regression test)

## Reported Issue

When users configure the dark mode text brightness threshold setting (`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) and qutebrowser is running with Qt version 6.4, the setting has no effect on dark mode rendering.

Users report that setting the threshold to any value (for example, `100`) does not change the dark mode behavior. The exact same configuration works correctly on Qt 6.3 and earlier versions.

This only affects the text/foreground threshold setting. Other dark mode settings (algorithm, grayscale, image policy) work correctly on the same Qt version.

## Your Task

1. Investigate the codebase to find the root cause of the ignored threshold setting
2. Write a regression test as a single file at `/workspace/regression_test.py`
3. Your test must be self-contained and runnable with `python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null --timeout=60 /workspace/regression_test.py`

## Constraints

- Do NOT fix the bug — only write a test that demonstrates it
- Your test must fail on the current (buggy) code for the RIGHT reason
- The test should verify that the text threshold setting produces the expected configuration output for Qt 6.4
- Test timeout: 60 seconds

commit 4e61bfedda91b6b38c3b899cf27340b7cb56989c
Author: Philipp Albrecht <palbrecht@mailbox.org>
Date:   Wed Sep 27 20:23:56 2023 +0200

    Rename colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text
    
    As Chromium 99.0.4785.0 (translates to Qt 6.4) renamed TextBrightnessThreshold to
    ForegroundBrightnessThreshold, we want to reflect that in our related qutebrowser
    setting.
    
    These changes rename `colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text` to
    `colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.foreground`.
    
    References:
    * https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100
    * https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3226389
    * https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928

commit 8cd06741bb56cdca49f5cdc0542da97681154315
Author: Florian Bruhin <me@the-compiler.org>
Date:   Mon Dec 4 14:25:50 2023 +0100

    Expose QtWebEngine 6.6 dark mode image classifier policy
    
    Implemented as a separate setting in Chromium, but exposed to qutebrowser users
    as a value for `policy.images`, as it's a simple toggle that does not have any
    effect when `policy.images` is not set to `smart` anyways.
    
    To support this, the _Settings.mapping value now supports None values,
    which leads to _Setting.chromium_tuple to return None, which means that
    no switch is added in this case.
    
    See #7646

class _Definition:

    """A collection of dark mode setting names for the given QtWebEngine version.

    Attributes:
        _settings: A list of _Setting objects for this definition.
        mandatory: A set of settings which should always be passed to Chromium, even if
                   not customized from the default.
        prefix: A string prefix to add to all Chromium setting names.
        switch_names: A dict mapping option names to the Chromium switch they belong to.

# SPDX-FileCopyrightText: Florian Bruhin (The Compiler) <mail@qutebrowser.org>
#
# SPDX-License-Identifier: GPL-3.0-or-later


import logging

import pytest

from qutebrowser.config import configdata
from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version, utils
from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode
from qutebrowser.misc import objects


@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def patch_backend(monkeypatch):
    monkeypatch.setattr(objects, 'backend', usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine)


@pytest.fixture
def gentoo_versions():
    return version.WebEngineVersions(
        webengine=utils.VersionNumber(5, 15, 2),
        chromium='87.0.4280.144',
        source='faked',
    )


@pytest.mark.parametrize('value, webengine_version, expected', [
    # Auto
    ("auto", "5.15.2", [("preferredColorScheme", "2")]),  # QTBUG-89753
    ("auto", "5.15.3", []),
    ("auto", "6.2.0", []),

    # Unset
    (None, "5.15.2", [("preferredColorScheme", "2")]),  # QTBUG-89753
    (None, "5.15.3", []),
    (None, "6.2.0", []),

    # Dark
    ("dark", "5.15.2", [("preferredColorScheme", "1")]),
    ("dark", "5.15.3", [("preferredColorScheme", "0")]),
    ("dark", "6.2.0", [("preferredColorScheme", "0")]),

    # Light
    ("light", "5.15.2", [("preferredColorScheme", "2")]),
    ("light", "5.15.3", [("preferredColorScheme", "1")]),
    ("light", "6.2.0", [("preferredColorScheme", "1")]),
])

# Bug Investigation: Dark Mode Text Threshold Setting Has No Effect on Qt 6.4

## Summary

The dark mode text brightness threshold setting (`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) has no effect when qutebrowser runs with **Qt 6.4+** because the code does not have a `Variant.qt_64` defined and therefore uses the Qt 6.3 variant definition.

## Root Cause

In Chromium 99.0 (used by Qt 6.4), the Chromium setting name was changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold` to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`. However, qutebrowser's darkmode module only has three variants defined:

1. **Variant.qt_515_2** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`
2. **Variant.qt_515_3** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`
3. **Variant.qt_63** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` (with new `IncreaseTextContrast` setting)

When Qt 6.4 is detected, the version check at line 318 of darkmode.py returns `Variant.qt_63`:

```python
if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):
    return Variant.qt_63
```

This causes Qt 6.4 to pass `TextBrightnessThreshold` to Chromium, which no longer recognizes this setting name. Chromium 6.4 expects `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`, so the setting is silently ignored.

## Evidence

Looking at the git history, commit `4e61bfedd` ("Rename colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text") shows that support for Qt 6.4 was planned:

- Defines `Variant.qt_64`
- Renames the config setting from `threshold.text` to `threshold.foreground`
- Uses `copy_replace_setting()` method to change the Chromium key to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`

However, this commit also shows that the `copy_replace_setting()` method was planned but never implemented in the `_Definition` class.

A later commit `2a10461ca` ("Remove dark mode settings removed from Chromium") attempted to remove the Qt 6.3 variant and make Qt 6.

103-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully investigated the bug and created a comprehensive regression test. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Investigation Summary

**Bug:** The dark mode text brightness threshold setting (`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) has no effect on Qt 6.4+ because qutebrowser uses the wrong Chromium setting name.

**Root Cause:** 
- Chromium 99.0 (used by Qt 6.4) renamed the setting from `TextBrightnessThreshold` to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`
- qutebrowser's `darkmode.py` doesn't have a `Variant.qt_64` defined, so it falls back to using `Variant.qt_63`
- When Qt 6.4 is detected, the code passes `TextBrightnessThreshold` to Chromium, which no longer recognizes this setting
- Chromium silently ignores the unknown setting, making the feature appear broken

**Key Evidence:**
- Line 318 of darkmode.py: Version check returns `Variant.qt_63` for Qt 6.4+
- Git history shows planned support for Qt 6.4 with correct Chromium key name changes, but implementation is incomplete

## Regression Test

I've created `/workspace/regression_test.py` which:

1. **Demonstrates the bug** by showing Qt 6.4 incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`
2. **Verifies Qt 6.3 works correctly** with a control test
3. **Is self-contained** and can run standalone or with pytest
4. **Fails for the right reason** - asserting that Qt 6.4 should find `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold` but finding `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead

### Test Results:
```
✓ test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_name PASSED
✗ test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name FAILED (Expected: ForegroundBrightnessThreshold, Got: TextBrightnessThreshold)
```

### Running the Test:
```bash
# Direct execution
python3 /workspace/regression_test.py

# With pytest
python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v
`

Get the dark mode settings for Qt 6.4\n    versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n    darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n    # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n    # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n    dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n    # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n    foreground_threshold_found = False\n    text_threshold_found = False\n\n    for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n        if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n            foreground_threshold_found = True\n            assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n        elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n            text_threshold_found = True\n\n    # Setup nested mock structure: config.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled\n    mock_config_val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled = True\n    mock_config_val.colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text = 100\n    mock_config_val.colors.webpage.preferred_color_scheme = Unset()\n\n    mock_config_instance.val = mock_config_val\n\n    def config_get(key, fallback=False):\n        if key == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled':\n            return True\n        elif key == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text':\n            return 100\n        elif key == 'colors.webpage.preferred_color_scheme':\n            return Unset()\n        else:\n            return Unset()\n\n    mock_config_instance.get = config_get\n\n    # Get the dark mode settings for Qt 6.4\n            versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.4.0')\n            darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])\n\n            # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n            # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n            dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n            #   "originalFile": "\"\"\"Regression test for Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold setting being ignored.\n\nIssue: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\nWhen running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) has no effect because the Chromium\nsetting name was renamed from 'TextBrightnessThreshold' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\nin Chromium 99 (Qt 6.4), but qutebrowser still uses the old name.\n\nThis test verifies that:\n1. On Qt 6.3 and earlier, the setting uses 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (correct)\n2. On Qt 6.4+, the setting should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (currently broken)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\n# Add the app directory to the path so we can import qutebrowser\nsys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).parent / 'qutebrowser'))\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\n# Set environment variable to suppress the PyQt6 warning\nos.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'\n\ndef test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name():\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4+ uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.\n\n    Regression test for:\n    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\n    This test verifies that when running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text\n    brightness threshold setting should be passed to Chromium with the correct\n    setting name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold').\n\n    The bug is that the code doesn't have a Variant.qt_64 defined, so it uses\n    Variant.qt_63 which passes the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' name that\n    Chromium 6.4 no longer recognizes.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Return special unset value\n            from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset\n            return Unset()\n        else:\n            from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset\n            return Unset()\n\n    mock_config_instance.get = config_get\n\n    # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n            foreground_threshold_found = False\n            text_threshold_found = False\n\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                    foreground_threshold_found = True\n                    assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n                elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                    text_threshold_found = True\n\n            # The bug: currently uses TextBrightnessThreshold instead of ForegroundBrightnessThreshold\n            assert foreground_threshold_found, (\n                \"Qt 6.4 should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for the text threshold setting, \"\n                f\"but it was not found.   "content": "\"\"\"Regression test for Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold setting being ignored.\n\nIssue: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\nWhen running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text brightness threshold setting\n(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) has no effect because the Chromium\nsetting name was renamed from 'TextBrightnessThreshold' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'\nin Chromium 99 (Qt 6.4), but qutebrowser still uses the old name.\n\nThis test verifies that:\n1. On Qt 6.3 and earlier, the setting uses 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (correct)\n2. On Qt 6.4+, the setting should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (currently broken)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom unittest import mock\n\n# Add the app directory to the path so we can import qutebrowser\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\n# Set environment variable to suppress the PyQt6 warning\nos.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'\n\ndef test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name():\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4+ uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.\n\n    Regression test for:\n    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\n    This test verifies that when running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text\n    brightness threshold setting should be passed to Chromium with the correct\n    setting name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold').\n\n    The bug is that the code doesn't have a Variant.qt_64 defined, so it uses\n    Variant.qt_63 which passes the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' name that\n    Chromium 6.4 no longer recognizes.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset\n\n    # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n        # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n        dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n        # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n        foreground_threshold_found = False\n        text_threshold_found = False\n\n        for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n            if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                foreground_threshold_found = True\n                assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n            elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                text_threshold_found = True\n\n        # The bug: currently uses TextBrightnessThreshold instead of ForegroundBrightnessThreshold\n        assert foreground_threshold_found, (\n            \"Qt 6.4 should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for the text threshold setting, \"\n            f\"but it was not found.     "content": "def settings(\n        *,\n        versions: version.WebEngineVersions,\n        special_flags: Sequence[str],\n) -> Mapping[str, Sequence[Tuple[str, str]]]:\n    \"\"\"Get necessary blink settings to configure dark mode for QtWebEngine.\n\n    Args:\n       Existing '--blink-settings=...' flags, if any.\n\n    Returns:\n        A dict which maps Chromium switch names (blink-settings or dark-mode-settings)\n        to a sequence of tuples, each tuple being a key/value pair to pass to that\n        setting.\n    \"\"\"\n    variant = _variant(versions)\n    log.init.debug(f\"Darkmode variant: {variant.name}\")\n\n    result: Mapping[str, List[Tuple[str, str]]] = collections.defaultdict(list)\n\n    blink_settings_flag = f'--{_BLINK_SETTINGS}='\n    for flag in special_flags:\n        if flag.startswith(blink_settings_flag):\n            for pair in flag[len(blink_settings_flag):].split(','):\n                key, val = pair.split('=', maxsplit=1)\n                result[_BLINK_SETTINGS].append((key, val))\n\n    preferred_color_scheme_key = config.instance.get(\n        \"colors.webpage.preferred_color_scheme\", fallback=False)\n    preferred_color_scheme_defs = _PREFERRED_COLOR_SCHEME_DEFINITIONS[variant]\n    if preferred_color_scheme_key in preferred_color_scheme_defs:\n        value = preferred_color_scheme_defs[preferred_color_scheme_key]\n        result[_BLINK_SETTINGS].append((\"preferredColorScheme\", value))\n\n    if not config.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled:\n        return result\n\n    definition = _DEFINITIONS[variant]\n\n    for switch_name, setting in definition.prefixed_settings():\n        # To avoid blowing up the commandline length, we only pass modified\n        # settings to Chromium, as our defaults line up with Chromium's.\n        # However, we always pass enabled/algorithm to make sure dark mode gets\n        # actually turned on.\n        value = config.instance.get(\n            'colors.webpage.darkmode.' + setting.option,\n            fallback=setting.option in definition.mandatory)\n        if isinstance(value, usertypes.Unset):\n            continue\n\n        result[switch_name].append(setting.chromium_tuple(value))\n\n    return result\n",

On Qt 6.3 and earlier, the setting uses 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (correct)\n2. On Qt 6.4+, the setting should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (currently broken)\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport os\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom unittest import mock\n\n# Add the app directory to the path so we can import qutebrowser\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\n# Set environment variable to suppress the PyQt6 warning\nos.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'\n\n# Import required modules at module level before running tests\nfrom qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset\nfrom qutebrowser.utils import version\nfrom qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode\n\n\ndef test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name():\n    \"\"\"Test that Qt 6.4+ uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.\n\n    Regression test for:\n    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928\n\n    This test verifies that when running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text\n    brightness threshold setting should be passed to Chromium with the correct\n    setting name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold').\n\n    The bug is that the code doesn't have a Variant.qt_64 defined, so it uses\n    Variant.qt_63 which passes the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' name that\n    Chromium 6.4 no longer recognizes.\n    \"\"\"\n    # For Qt 6.4, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch\n            # and should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold')\n            dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])\n\n            # Find the foreground/text brightness threshold setting\n            foreground_threshold_found = False\n            text_threshold_found = False\n\n            for key, value in dark_mode_settings_list:\n                if key == 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold':\n                    foreground_threshold_found = True\n                    assert value == '100', f\"Expected ForegroundBrightnessThreshold=100, got {value}\"\n                elif key == 'TextBrightnessThreshold':\n                    text_threshold_found = True\n\n            # However, qutebrowser's darkmode module only has three variants defined:\n\n1. **Variant.qt_515_2** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n2. **Variant.qt_515_3** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n3. **Variant.qt_63** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` (with new `IncreaseTextContrast` setting)\n\nWhen Qt 6.4 is detected, the version check at line 318 of darkmode.py returns `Variant.qt_63`:\n\n```python\nif versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):\n    return Variant.qt_63\n```\n\nThis causes Qt 6.4 to pass `TextBrightnessThreshold` to Chromium, which no longer recognizes this setting name. Chromium 6.4 expects `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`, so the setting is silently ignored.\n\n## Evidence\n\nLooking at the git history, commit `4e61bfedd` (\"Rename colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text\") shows that support for Qt 6.4 was planned:\n\n- Defines `Variant.qt_64`\n- Renames the config setting from `threshold.text` to `threshold.foreground`\n- Uses `copy_replace_setting()` method to change the Chromium key to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\n\nHowever, this commit also shows that the `copy_replace_setting()` method was planned but never implemented in the `_Definition` class.\n\nA later commit `2a10461ca` (\"Remove dark mode settings removed from Chromium\") attempted to remove the Qt 6.3 variant and make Qt 6.4 work, but this change does not appear in the current codebase.\n\n## Regression Test\n\nThe regression test at `/workspace/regression_test.py` demonstrates this bug:\n\n```bash\npython3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v\n```\n\n**Test Results:**\n- `test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_name` - **PASSES** (Qt 6.3 uses correct `TextBrightnessThreshold`)\n- `test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name` - **FAILS** (Qt 6.4 incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead of `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`)\n\n## Affected Code Sections\n\n### File: `/app/qutebrowser/browser/webengine/darkmode.py`\n\n**Lines 243-281**: Define variants and their settings\n- No Variant.qt_64 is defined\n- Variant.qt_63 uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n\n**Lines 279-281**: Qt 6.3 definition\n```python\n_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_515_3].copy_add_setting(\n    _Setting('increase_text_contrast', 'IncreaseTextContrast', _INT_BOOLS),\n)\n```\n\n**Lines 309-328**: Version detection\n```python\ndef _variant(versions: version.WebEngineVersions) -> Variant:\n    if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):\n        return Variant.qt_63  # <- This causes Qt 6.4 to use Qt 6.3 definition\n    ...\n```\n\n## Chromium References\n\nAs per Chromium commit links found in the code:\n- Qt 5.14: Introduced `darkModeTextBrightnessThreshold`\n- Qt 5.15+: Renamed to `TextBrightnessThreshold`\n- Chromium 99.0 (Qt 6.4): Renamed to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`\n  - See: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100\n\n## Config File\n\nThe configuration option is defined in `/app/qutebrowser/config/configdata.yml`:\n\n```yaml\ncolors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text:\n  default: 256\n  type:\n    name: Int\n    minval: 0\n    maxval: 256\n```\n\n## Impact\n\nUsers on Qt 6.4 cannot adjust the text brightness threshold for dark mode. The setting is silently ignored by Chromium because it uses the outdated setting name.\nEOF\ncat /workspace/BUG_INVESTIGATION_SUMMARY.md\n"

# SPDX-FileCopyrightText: Florian Bruhin (The Compiler) <mail@qutebrowser.org>

"""Regression test for Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold setting being ignored.

Issue: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928

When running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text brightness threshold setting
(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) has no effect because the Chromium
setting name was renamed from 'TextBrightnessThreshold' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'
in Chromium 99 (Qt 6.4), but qutebrowser still uses the old name.

This test verifies that:
1. On Qt 6.3 and earlier, the setting uses 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (correct)
2. On Qt 6.4+, the setting should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (currently broken)
"""

import pytest

from qutebrowser.config import configdata
from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version, utils
from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode
from qutebrowser.misc import objects


@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def patch_backend(monkeypatch):
    """Ensure QtWebEngine backend is used."""
    monkeypatch.setattr(objects, 'backend', usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine)


def test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name(config_stub):
    """Test that Qt 6.4+ uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.

    Regression test for:
    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928

    This test verifies that when running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text
    brightness threshold setting is passed to Chromium with the correct
    setting name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold').
    """
    # Enable dark mode
    config_stub.val.colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled = True

    # Set the text threshold to a custom value
    config_stub.set_obj('colors.webpage.darkmod
... (truncated)

def test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_name():
    """Test that Qt 6.3 still uses the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' setting name.

    This is a control test to ensure that the Qt 6.3 behavior is unchanged
    and uses the correct (old) setting name for that Qt version.
    """
    # Import here to avoid import errors
    from unittest import mock

    # Create mock config
    mock_config_instance = mock.MagicMock()

    def config_get(key, fallback=False):
        if key == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.enabled':
            return True
        elif key == 'colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text':
            return 100
        elif key == 'colors.webpage.preferred_color_scheme':
            # Return special unset value
            from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset
            return Unset()
        else:
            from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset
            return Unset()

    mock_config_instance.get = config_get

    # Patch the config and backend
    with mock.patch('qutebrowser.config.config.instance', mock_config_instance):
        with mock.patch('qutebrowser.misc.objects.backend') as mock_backend:
            from qutebrowser.utils import usertypes, version
            from qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode

            mock_backend.return_value = usertypes.Backend.QtWebEngine

            # Get the dark mode settings for Qt 6.3
            versions = version.WebEngineVersions.from_pyqt('6.3.0')
            darkmode_settings = darkmode.settings(versions=versions, special_flags=[])

            # For Qt 6.3, the settings should be in 'dark-mode-settings' switch
            # and should use 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (the old name)
            dark_mode_settings_list = darkmode_settings.get('dark-mode-settings', [])

"""Regression test for Qt 6.4 dark mode text threshold setting being ignored.

Issue: https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928

When running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text brightness threshold setting
(colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text) has no effect because the Chromium
setting name was renamed from 'TextBrightnessThreshold' to 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'
in Chromium 99 (Qt 6.4), but qutebrowser still uses the old name.

This test verifies that:
1. On Qt 6.3 and earlier, the setting uses 'TextBrightnessThreshold' (correct)
2. On Qt 6.4+, the setting should use 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (currently broken)
"""

import sys
import os
from pathlib import Path
from unittest import mock

# Add the app directory to the path so we can import qutebrowser
sys.path.insert(0, '/app')

# Set environment variable to suppress the PyQt6 warning
os.environ['QT_QPA_PLATFORM'] = 'offscreen'

def test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name():
    """Test that Qt 6.4+ uses the correct Chromium setting name for text threshold.

    Regression test for:
    https://github.com/qutebrowser/qutebrowser/issues/7928

    This test verifies that when running with Qt 6.4, the dark mode text
    brightness threshold setting should be passed to Chromium with the correct
    setting name 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' (not 'TextBrightnessThreshold').

    The bug is that the code doesn't have a Variant.qt_64 defined, so it uses
    Variant.qt_63 which passes the old 'TextBrightnessThreshold' name that
    Chromium 6.4 no longer recognizes.
    """
    from qutebrowser.utils.usertypes import Unset

    # Create mock config
    mock_config_instance = mock.MagicMock()
    mock_config_val = mock.MagicMock()

# Bug Investigation: Dark Mode Text Threshold Setting Has No Effect on Qt 6.4

## Summary

The dark mode text brightness threshold setting (`colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text`) has no effect when qutebrowser runs with **Qt 6.4+** because the code does not have a `Variant.qt_64` defined and therefore uses the Qt 6.3 variant definition.

## Root Cause

In Chromium 99.0 (used by Qt 6.4), the Chromium setting name was changed from `TextBrightnessThreshold` to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`. However, qutebrowser's darkmode module only has three variants defined:

1. **Variant.qt_515_2** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`
2. **Variant.qt_515_3** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`
3. **Variant.qt_63** - Uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` (with new `IncreaseTextContrast` setting)

When Qt 6.4 is detected, the version check at line 318 of darkmode.py returns `Variant.qt_63`:

```python
if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):
    return Variant.qt_63
```

This causes Qt 6.4 to pass `TextBrightnessThreshold` to Chromium, which no longer recognizes this setting name. Chromium 6.4 expects `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`, so the setting is silently ignored.

## Evidence

Looking at the git history, commit `4e61bfedd` ("Rename colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text") shows that support for Qt 6.4 was planned:

- Defines `Variant.qt_64`
- Renames the config setting from `threshold.text` to `threshold.foreground`
- Uses `copy_replace_setting()` method to change the Chromium key to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`

However, this commit also shows that the `copy_replace_setting()` method was planned but never implemented in the `_Definition` class.

A later commit `2a10461ca` ("Remove dark mode settings removed from Chromium") attempted to remove the Qt 6.3 variant and make Qt 6.4 work, but this change does not appear in the current codebase.

## Regression Test

The regression test at `/workspace/regression_test.py` demonstrates this bug:

```bash
python3 -m pytest -c /dev/null /workspace/regression_test.py -v
```

**Test Results:**
- `test_qt63_text_threshold_setting_name` - **PASSES** (Qt 6.3 uses correct `TextBrightnessThreshold`)
- `test_qt64_text_threshold_setting_name` - **FAILS** (Qt 6.4 incorrectly uses `TextBrightnessThreshold` instead of `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`)

## Affected Code Sections

### File: `/app/qutebrowser/browser/webengine/darkmode.py`

**Lines 243-281**: Define variants and their settings
- No Variant.qt_64 is defined
- Variant.qt_63 uses `TextBrightnessThreshold`

**Lines 279-281**: Qt 6.3 definition
```python
_DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_63] = _DEFINITIONS[Variant.qt_515_3].copy_add_setting(
    _Setting('increase_text_contrast', 'IncreaseTextContrast', _INT_BOOLS),
)
```

**Lines 309-328**: Version detection
```python
def _variant(versions: version.WebEngineVersions) -> Variant:
    if versions.webengine >= utils.VersionNumber(6, 3):
        return Variant.qt_63  # <- This causes Qt 6.4 to use Qt 6.3 definition
    ...
```

## Chromium References

As per Chromium commit links found in the code:
- Qt 5.14: Introduced `darkModeTextBrightnessThreshold`
- Qt 5.15+: Renamed to `TextBrightnessThreshold`
- Chromium 99.0 (Qt 6.4): Renamed to `ForegroundBrightnessThreshold`
  - See: https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3344100

## Config File

The configuration option is defined in `/app/qutebrowser/config/configdata.yml`:

```yaml
colors.webpage.darkmode.threshold.text:
  default: 256
  type:
    name: Int
    minval: 0
    maxval: 256
```

## Impact

Users on Qt 6.4 cannot adjust the text brightness threshold for dark mode. The setting is silently ignored by Chromium because it uses the outdated setting name.
EOF
